color:black;"> </span> 18–23</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ffa020; color:black;"> </span> 24–32</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff9a20; color:black;"> </span> 33–43</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#f08015; color:black;"> </span> 44–50</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#e06815; color:black;"> </span> 51–66</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#d85010; color:black;"> </span> 67–95</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#d02010; color:white;"> </span> 96–251</div></div>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 285px"><div style="width: 285px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 280px;"><div style="margin:20px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg" title="Disability-adjusted life year for asthma per 100,000 inhabitants in 2004.[269]   no data   0-100   100–150   150–200   200–250   250–300   300–350   350–400   400–450   450–500   500–550   550–600   &gt;600"><img alt="A map of the world with Europe shaded yellow, most of North and South America orange and Southern Africa a dark red" data-file-height="415" data-file-width="940" decoding="async" height="110" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg/250px-Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg/375px-Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg/500px-Asthma_world_map_-_DALY_-_WHO2004.svg.png 2x" width="250"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<a href="/wiki/Disability-adjusted_life_year" title="Disability-adjusted life year">Disability-adjusted life year</a> for asthma per 100,000 inhabitants in 2004.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-269"><a href="#cite_note-269">[269]</a></sup><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1054258005" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="refbegin refbegin-columns references-column-count references-column-count-3" style="column-count: 3;"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#b3b3b3; color:black;"> </span> no data</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ffff65; color:black;"> </span> 0-100</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#fff200; color:black;"> </span> 100–150</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ffdc00; color:black;"> </span> 150–200</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ffc600; color:black;"> </span> 200–250</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ffb000; color:black;"> </span> 250–300</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff9a00; color:black;"> </span> 300–350</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff8400; color:black;"> </span> 350–400</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff6e00; color:black;"> </span> 400–450</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff5800; color:black;"> </span> 450–500</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff4200; color:black;"> </span> 500–550</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#ff2c00; color:black;"> </span> 550–600</div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="legend"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#cb0000; color:white;"> </span> &gt;600</div></div>
</div>
</div></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Epidemiology">Epidemiology</span></h2>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Epidemiology_of_asthma" title="Epidemiology of asthma">Epidemiology of asthma</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Asthma_prevalence,_OWID.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="850" decoding="async" height="247" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Asthma_prevalence%2C_OWID.svg/350px-Asthma_prevalence%2C_OWID.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Asthma_prevalence%2C_OWID.svg/525px-Asthma_prevalence%2C_OWID.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Asthma_prevalence%2C_OWID.svg/700px-Asthma_prevalence%2C_OWID.svg.png 2x" width="350"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Asthma_prevalence,_OWID.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rates of asthma in 2017<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-270"><a href="#cite_note-270">[270]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p>In 2019, approximately 262 million people worldwide were affected by asthma and approximately 461,000 people died from the disease.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lancetasthma_9-3"><a href="#cite_note-lancetasthma-9">[9]</a></sup> Rates vary between countries with prevalences between 1 and 18%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GINA2011p2_22-3"><a href="#cite_note-GINA2011p2-22">[22]</a></sup> It is more common in <a href="/wiki/Developed_country" title="Developed country">developed</a> than <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Developing_countries" title="Developing countries">developing countries</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GINA2011p2_22-4"><a href="#cite_note-GINA2011p2-22">[22]</a></sup> One thus sees lower rates in Asia, Eastern Europe and Africa.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M38_21-10"><a href="#cite_note-M38-21">[21]</a></sup> Within developed countries it is more common in those who are economically disadvantaged while in contrast in developing countries it is more common in the affluent.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GINA2011p2_22-5"><a href="#cite_note-GINA2011p2-22">[22]</a></sup> The reason for these differences is not well known.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GINA2011p2_22-6"><a href="#cite_note-GINA2011p2-22">[22]</a></sup> Low and middle income countries make up more than 80% of the mortality.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-271"><a href="#cite_note-271">[271]</a></sup>
</p><p>While asthma is twice as common in boys as girls,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GINA2011p2_22-7"><a href="#cite_note-GINA2011p2-22">[22]</a></sup> severe asthma occurs at equal rates.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bush2009_272-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bush2009-272">[272]</a></sup> In contrast adult women have a higher rate of asthma than men<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GINA2011p2_22-8"><a href="#cite_note-GINA2011p2-22">[22]</a></sup> and it is more common in the young than the old.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M38_21-11"><a href="#cite_note-M38-21">[21]</a></sup> In 2010, children with asthma experienced over 900,000 emergency department visits, making it the most common reason for admission to the hospital following an emergency department visit in the US in 2011.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-273"><a href="#cite_note-273">[273]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-274"><a href="#cite_note-274">[274]</a></sup>
</p><p>Global rates of asthma have increased significantly between the 1960s and 2008<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ana2010_19-1"><a href="#cite_note-Ana2010-19">[19]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-275"><a href="#cite_note-275">[275]</a></sup> with it being recognized as a major public health problem since the 1970s.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M38_21-12"><a href="#cite_note-M38-21">[21]</a></sup> Rates of asthma have plateaued in the developed world since the mid-1990s with recent increases primarily in the developing world.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid16175830_276-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid16175830-276">[276]</a></sup> Asthma affects approximately 7% of the population of the United States<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fanta2009_195-1"><a href="#cite_note-Fanta2009-195">[195]</a></sup> and 5% of people in the United Kingdom.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Anderson2007_277-0"><a href="#cite_note-Anderson2007-277">[277]</a></sup> Canada, Australia and New Zealand have rates of about 14–15%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-278"><a href="#cite_note-278">[278]</a></sup>
</p><p>The average death rate from 2011 to 2015 from asthma in the UK was about 50% higher than the average for the European Union and had increased by about 5% in that time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-279"><a href="#cite_note-279">[279]</a></sup> Children are more likely see a physician due to asthma symptoms after school starts in September.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-280"><a href="#cite_note-280">[280]</a></sup>
</p><p>Population-based epidemiological studies describe temporal associations between acute respiratory illnesses, asthma, and development of severe asthma with irreversible airflow limitation (known as the asthma-chronic obstructive pulmonary disease "overlap" syndrome, or ACOS).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-281"><a href="#cite_note-281">[281]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-282"><a href="#cite_note-282">[282]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-283"><a href="#cite_note-283">[283]</a></sup> Additional prospective population-based data indicate that ACOS seems to represent a form of severe asthma, characterised by more frequent hospitalisations, and to be the result of early-onset asthma that has progressed to fixed airflow obstruction.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-284"><a href="#cite_note-284">[284]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economics">Economics</span></h2>
<p>From 2000 to 2010, the average cost per asthma-related hospital stay in the United States for children remained relatively stable at about $3,600, whereas the average cost per asthma-related hospital stay for adults increased from $5,200 to $6,600.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USEco2014_285-0"><a href="#cite_note-USEco2014-285">[285]</a></sup> In 2010, Medicaid was the most frequent primary payer among children and adults aged 18–44 years in the United States; private insurance was the second most frequent payer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USEco2014_285-1"><a href="#cite_note-USEco2014-285">[285]</a></sup> Among both children and adults in the lowest income communities in the United States there is a higher rate of hospital stays for asthma in 2010 than those in the highest income communities.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USEco2014_285-2"><a href="#cite_note-USEco2014-285">[285]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Papyrus_Ebers.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="308" decoding="async" height="286" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Papyrus_Ebers.png/220px-Papyrus_Ebers.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c5/Papyrus_Ebers.png 1.5x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Papyrus_Ebers.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Ebers_Papyrus" title="Ebers Papyrus">Ebers Papyrus</a></i> detailing treatment of asthma</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1246" data-file-width="711" decoding="async" height="298" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg/170px-Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg/255px-Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg/340px-Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Grimaults_cigarette_ad.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>1907 advertisement for Grimault's Indian Cigarettes, promoted as a means of relieving asthma. They contained <a href="/wiki/Atropa_belladonna" title="Atropa belladonna">belladonna</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cannabis" title="Cannabis">cannabis</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Asthma was recognized in <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Egypt" title="Ancient Egypt">ancient Egypt</a> and was treated by drinking an <a href="/wiki/Incense" title="Incense">incense</a> mixture known as <a href="/wiki/Kyphi" title="Kyphi">kyphi</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manniche1999_20-1"><a href="#cite_note-Manniche1999-20">[20]</a></sup> It was officially named as a specific respiratory problem by <a href="/wiki/Hippocrates" title="Hippocrates">Hippocrates</a> circa 450 BC, with the Greek word for "panting" forming the basis of our modern name.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M38_21-13"><a href="#cite_note-M38-21">[21]</a></sup> In 200 BC it was believed to be at least partly related to the emotions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Andrew2010_29-1"><a href="#cite_note-Andrew2010-29">[29]</a></sup> In the 12th century the Jewish physician-philosopher <a href="/wiki/Maimonides" title="Maimonides">Maimonides</a> wrote a treatise on asthma in Arabic, based partly on Arabic sources, in which he discussed the symptoms, proposed various dietary and other means of treatment, and emphasized the importance of climate and clean air.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-286"><a href="#cite_note-286">[286]</a></sup>
</p><p>In 1873, one of the first papers in modern medicine on the subject tried to explain the <a href="/wiki/Pathophysiology" title="Pathophysiology">pathophysiology</a> of the disease while one in 1872, concluded that asthma can be cured by rubbing the chest with <a href="/wiki/A.B.C._Liniment" title="A.B.C. Liniment">chloroform liniment</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid20747287_287-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid20747287-287">[287]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid20746575_288-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid20746575-288">[288]</a></sup> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pharmaceutical_drug" title="Pharmaceutical drug">Medical treatment</a> in 1880 included the use of <a href="/wiki/Intravenous_therapy" title="Intravenous therapy">intravenous</a> doses of a drug called <a href="/wiki/Pilocarpine" title="Pilocarpine">pilocarpine</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid20749537_289-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid20749537-289">[289]</a></sup> In 1886, F. H. Bosworth theorized a connection between asthma and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hay_fever" title="Hay fever">hay fever</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid21407325_290-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid21407325-290">[290]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Epinephrine_(medication)" title="Epinephrine (medication)">Epinephrine</a> was first referred to in the treatment of asthma in 1905.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid18733372_291-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid18733372-291">[291]</a></sup> Oral corticosteroids began to be used for this condition in the 1950s while inhaled corticosteroids and selective short acting beta agonist came into wide use in the 1960s.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid22375974_292-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid22375974-292">[292]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid17092772_293-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid17092772-293">[293]</a></sup>
</p><p>A well-documented case in the 19th century was that of young <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt#Early_life_and_family" title="Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a> (1858–1919). At that time there was no effective treatment. Roosevelt's youth was in large part shaped by his poor health partly related to his asthma. He experienced recurring nighttime asthma attacks that felt as if he was being smothered to death, terrifying the boy and his parents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-294"><a href="#cite_note-294">[294]</a></sup>
</p><p>During the 1930s to 1950s, asthma was known as one of the "holy seven" <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Psychosomatic_illness" title="Psychosomatic illness">psychosomatic illnesses</a>. Its cause was considered to be psychological, with treatment often based on psychoanalysis and other <a href="/wiki/Talking_cure" title="Talking cure">talking cures</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid16185365_295-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid16185365-295">[295]</a></sup> As these psychoanalysts interpreted the asthmatic wheeze as the suppressed cry of the child for its mother, they considered the treatment of depression to be especially important for individuals with asthma.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid16185365_295-1"><a href="#cite_note-pmid16185365-295">[295]</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2021, an appeal court in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> overturned a deportation order against a 40-year-old Bangladeshi man, who was a patient of asthma. His lawyers had argued that the dangerous levels of <a href="/wiki/Pollution" title="Pollution">pollution</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> could possibly lead to worsening of his health condition, or even premature death.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-296"><a href="#cite_note-296">[296]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
